        var reg = new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]*)(;|$)')
        var r = document.cookie.match(reg)
        return r ? unescape(r[2]) : null
      }

      function handleDocumentInitActive() {
        setTimeout(function () {
          if (!(history.state && history.state.back)) {
            var now = (Date.now() + '').substr(-8)
            var url = document.URL
            var qsIdx = url.indexOf('?')
            if (!~qsIdx) {
              url = url + '?vt=' + now
            } else if (/vt=\d{8}/.test(url)) {
              url = url.replace(/vt=\d{8}/, 'vt=' + now)
            } else {
              var suffix = url.substring(qsIdx + 1)
              url = url.substring(0, qsIdx + 1) + 'vt=' + now
              if (suffix) url = url + '&' + suffix
            }
            history.pushState(null, document.title, url)
          }
        }, 300)
        document.removeEventListener('click', handleDocumentInitActive)
      }
